49 /*
50 * A brief explanation of how this works:
51 *
52 * Each property name is a global variable of a unique type. That type has
53 * an inner class template instantiated by its operator=. For instance,
54 * the property checked is an instance of checkedProp, and checked=true
55 * returns an instance of checkedProp::Value<bool>.
56 *
57 * The builder classes have a generic applyProp function that rejects any
58 * argument as invalid. ZCGUI_ACCEPT_PROP adds a specialization for that
59 * property that calls the corresponding function on the widget. Similarly,
60 * the builders have an addChildren function that rejects all children.
61 * ZCGUI_ACCEPT_ONE_CHILD and ZCGUI_ACCEPT_MULTIPLE_CHILDREN add overloads
62 * that call the appropriate functions.
63 *
64 * A builder function calls the corresponding makeX function and creates
65 * a builder class, then passes everything to the applyArgs functions.
66 * If the first argument is a property, it calls the builder's applyProp
67 * function and calls applyArgs with the remaining arguments. If it's a widget
68 * pointer, it passes all the remaining arguments to addChildren.
69 */
70

542 #define _d DummyWidget()
543
544 #define INITD_ROW(ind, d_mem, lab_mem) \
545 Row(vPadding = 0_px, \
546 TextField(maxLength = 64, \
547 text = std::string(lab_mem[ind]), \
548 type = GUI::TextField::type::TEXT, \
549 width = 8_em, \
550 rightPadding = 0_px, \
551 onValChangedFunc = [&](GUI::TextField::type,std::string_view str,int32_t) \
552 { \
553 for(size_t q = 0; q < 65; ++q) \
554 { \
555 if(q < str.size()) \
556 lab_mem[ind][q] = str.at(q); \
557 else \
558 lab_mem[ind][q] = 0; \
559 } \
560 } \
561 ), \
562 TextField( \
563 type = GUI::TextField::type::SWAP_ZSINT, \
564 val = d_mem[ind], \
565 width = 6.5_em+16_px, \
566 leftPadding = 0_px, \
567 onValChangedFunc = [&](GUI::TextField::type,std::string_view,int32_t val) \
568 { \
569 d_mem[ind] = val; \
570 } \
571 ) \
572 )
573
574 #define INITD_ROW2(ind, d_mem) \
575 Row(vPadding = 0_px, \
576 Label( text = "InitD["+std::to_string(ind)+"]:", \
577 textAlign = 2, \
578 rightPadding = 0_px \
579 ), \
580 TextField( \
581 type = GUI::TextField::type::SWAP_ZSINT, \
582 val = d_mem[ind], \
583 width = 6.5_em+16_px, \
584 leftPadding = 0_px, \
585 onValChangedFunc = [&](GUI::TextField::type,std::string_view,int32_t val) \
586 { \
587 d_mem[ind] = val; \
588 } \
589 ) \
590 )
591
592 #define SCRIPT_LIST(name, list, mem) \
593 Label(minwidth = 6.5_em, text = name, textAlign = 2), \
594 DropDownList( \
595 fitParent = true, \
596 data = list, \
597 selectedValue = mem, \
598 onSelectFunc = [&](int32_t val) \
599 { \
600 mem = val; \
601 } \
602 )
603
604 #define SCRIPT_LIST_PROC(name, list, mem, proc) \
605 Label(minwidth = 6.5_em, text = name, textAlign = 2), \
606 DropDownList( \
607 fitParent = true, \
608 data = list, \
609 selectedValue = mem, \
610 onSelectFunc = [&](int32_t val) \
611 { \
612 mem = val; \
613 proc(); \
614 } \
615 )
